### Libyan civil war cleanup events ###
#Give the winner LBA cosmetic tag
country_event = {
	id = Libya.0

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = HOR
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = GNA
					has_war_with = GNC
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = GNA
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = HOR
					has_war_with = GNC
					has_cosmetic_tag = GNA_NTC
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = GNC
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = GNA
					has_war_with = HOR
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = Libya_Civil_War_Over }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	immediate = {
		#Civil war is over
		set_global_flag = Libya_Civil_War_Over
		#Clear core status
		391 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		392 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		393 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		395 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		396 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		397 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		579 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		919 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		918 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		920 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		1100 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		1101 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}

		#Make Winner Libya
		set_cosmetic_tag = LBA
		set_country_flag = dynamic_flag
		set_country_flag = dynamic_rebel_flag
		add_state_core = 391
		add_state_core = 392
		add_state_core = 393
		add_state_core = 395
		add_state_core = 396
		add_state_core = 397
		add_state_core = 918
		add_state_core = 919
		add_state_core = 920
		add_state_core = 579
		add_state_core = 1100
		add_state_core = 1101
		set_capital = { state = 391 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = Non_State_Actor }
			remove_ideas = Non_State_Actor
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = rival_government }
			remove_ideas = rival_government
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { threat_level = 30 }
		clamp_threat = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = Libya.0.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = LibyaNews.1 hours = 6 } }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Libya.0.a executed"
	}
}

#Recreate Libya in case Libya is annexed
country_event = {
	id = Libya.1

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			country_exists = LBA
			country_exists = HOR
			country_exists = GNC
			country_exists = GNA
		}
		NOT = { 391 = { is_core_of = LBA } }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	immediate = {
		#Clear core status
		391 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		392 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		393 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		395 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR
			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		396 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA
			remove_core_of = HOR

			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		397 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA

		}
		918 = {

			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		919 = {

			remove_core_of = GNA
			remove_core_of = GNC
		}
		920 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA

			remove_core_of = GNC
		}

		1100 = {
			remove_core_of = LBA

			add_state_core = 391

			add_state_core = 396
			add_state_core = 397

			add_state_core = 919
			add_state_core = 920
			add_state_core = 579
			add_state_core = 1100
			add_state_core = 1101
			set_capital = { state = 391 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = Libya.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Libya.1.a executed"
	}
}

news_event = {

	id = LibyaNews.1
	title = LibyaNews.1.t
	desc = {
		text = LibyaNews.1.GNA.d
		trigger = { FROM = { original_tag = GNA } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = LibyaNews.1.HOR.d
		trigger = { FROM = { original_tag = HOR } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = LibyaNews.1.GNC.d
		trigger = { FROM = { original_tag = GNC } }
	}
	picture = GFX_news_libyan_civil_war

	major = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaNews.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaNews.1.a executed"
	}

}

#############################
# FOCUS TREE RELATED EVENTS #
#############################
#Libya allies itself with Boko Haram
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFocus.1
	title = LibyaFocus.1.t
	desc = LibyaFocus.1.desc
	picture = GFX_boko_haram_insurgency

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.1.a executed"
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.10
		}
	}
}

#Boko Haram rises up because of Libya
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFocus.2
	title = LibyaFocus.2.t
	desc = LibyaFocus.2.desc
	picture = GFX_boko_haram_insurgency

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_temp_variable = { salafist_popularity = party_popularity@fascism }
		multiply_temp_variable = { salafist_popularity = 2 }
		clamp_temp_variable = { var = salafist_popularity max = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { opposition_popularity = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { opposition_popularity = salafist_popularity }
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.2.a		#Fight against Boko Haram
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.2.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = fascism
			size = salafist_popularity
			capital = 339
			states = { 338 339 340 }
			hidden_effect = {
				unlock_national_focus = NIG_rise_of_boko_haram
				add_ideas = NIG_islamic_majority_10_idea
				LBA = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV
						enemy = PREV.PREV
						hostility_reason = asked_to_join
					}
				}
			}
		}
		LBA = { country_event = { id = LibyaFocus.3 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.2.b		#Become Boko Haram
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.2.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_capital = { state = 339 }
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = ROOT
			ruling_party = fascism
			size = opposition_popularity
			states = { 336 337 334 332 }
			LBA = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = PREV.PREV
					enemy = PREV
					hostility_reason = asked_to_join
				}
			}
		}
		unlock_national_focus = NIG_rise_of_boko_haram
		add_ideas = NIG_islamic_majority_10_idea
		LBA = { country_event = { id = LibyaFocus.3 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Libya joins Nigerian civil war
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFocus.3
	title = LibyaFocus.3.t
	desc = LibyaFocus.3.desc
	picture = GFX_boko_haram_insurgency

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.3.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.3.a executed"
	}
}

## Rewriting the Green Book events
#1:1 - The Instrument Of Government
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFocus.4
	title = LibyaFocus.4.t
	desc = LibyaFocus.4.desc
	picture = GFX_message_signing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.4.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.4.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 33 }
		lba_increase_reform = yes
		set_temp_variable = { LBA_new_green_book_stability_effect_temp = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { LBA_new_green_book_stability_effect = LBA_new_green_book_stability_effect_temp }
		set_temp_variable = { LBA_new_green_book_political_power_effect_temp = -0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { LBA_new_green_book_political_power_effect = LBA_new_green_book_political_power_effect_temp }
		custom_effect_tooltip = libya_green_book_1_1_reform_effect_tt
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.4.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.4.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 33 }
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.4.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.4.c executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 33 }
		lba_decrease_reform = yes
		set_temp_variable = { LBA_new_green_book_stability_effect_temp = -0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { LBA_new_green_book_stability_effect = LBA_new_green_book_stability_effect_temp }
		set_temp_variable = { LBA_new_green_book_political_power_effect_temp = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { LBA_new_green_book_political_power_effect = LBA_new_green_book_political_power_effect_temp }
		custom_effect_tooltip = libya_green_book_1_1_reform_effect_tt
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	}
}

#2:16 - Land
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFocus.10
	title = LibyaFocus.10.t
	desc = LibyaFocus.10.desc
	picture = GFX_message_signing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.10.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.10.a executed"

country_event = {
	id = LibyaFocus.23
	title = LibyaFocus.23.t
	desc = LibyaFocus.23.d
	picture = GFX_fighter_jet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.23.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.23.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					arms_factory > 0
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					arms_factory > 0
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					offices > 0
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					offices > 0
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = offices
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					industrial_complex > 0
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					industrial_complex > 0
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					dockyard > 0
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					dockyard > 0
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 50
					random_list = {
						10 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_exile
									has_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dead
									has_country_leader = {
										name = "Muhammad Muammar Gaddafi"
										ruling_only = yes
									}
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = kill_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi
						}
						10 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = saif_al_islam_gaddafi_exile
									has_country_flag = saif_al_islam_gaddafi_dead
									has_country_leader = {
										name = "Saif al-Islam Gaddafi"
										ruling_only = yes
									}
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = kill_saif_al_islam_gaddafi
						}
						10 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = al_saadi_gaddafi_exile
									has_country_flag = al_saadi_gaddafi_dead
									has_country_leader = {
										name = "Al-Saadi Gaddafi"
										ruling_only = yes
									}
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = kill_al_saadi_gaddafi
						}
						10 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_exile
									has_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_dead
									has_country_leader = {
										name = "Mutassim Gaddafi"
										ruling_only = yes
									}
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = kill_mutassim_gaddafi
						}
						10 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = hannibal_gaddafi_exile
									has_country_flag = hannibal_gaddafi_dead
									has_country_leader = {
										name = "Hannibal Gaddafi"
										ruling_only = yes
									}
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = kill_hannibal_gaddafi
						}

									has_country_flag = saif_al_arab_gaddafi_dead

#Liberate minorities
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFocus.26
	title = LibyaFocus.26.t
	desc = LibyaFocus.26.d
	picture = GFX_liberate_minorities

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.26.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.26.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 1
				}
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				any_other_country = {
					has_guaranteed = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = { is_core_of = TIE }
				any_owned_state = { is_core_of = TUA }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = TIE
					NOT = { country_exists = TUA }
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = TIE
					}
					transfer_state_to = TIE
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = TUA
					NOT = { country_exists = TIE }
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = TUA
					}
					transfer_state_to = TUA
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = TUA
					country_exists = TIE
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = TIE
					}
					transfer_state_to = TIE
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = TUA
					}
					transfer_state_to = TUA
				}
			}
			else = {
				release = TIE
				FROM = { puppet = TIE }
				release = TUA
				FROM = { puppet = TUA }
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { any_owned_state = { is_core_of = TIE } }
				release = TIE
				FROM = { puppet = TIE }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_owned_state = { is_core_of = TUA } }
				release = TUA
				FROM = { puppet = TUA }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = LibyaFocus.27 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.26.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 1
				}
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				any_other_country = {
					has_guaranteed = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.26.b executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = LibyaFocus.28 hours = 6 } }
	}
}

		name = LibyaFocus.46.a

			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				same_ideology = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				LBA = { is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_relation_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = military_cooperation
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = FROM }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes } }
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = LibyaFocus.47 hours = 6 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.46.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.46.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				same_ideology = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				LBA = { is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}

country_event = {
	id = LibyaFocus.50
	title = LibyaFocus.50.t
	desc = LibyaFocus.50.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Money_ITA_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.50.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.50.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = nationalist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -5 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_political_power = 50
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = nationalist }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist
				popularity = -0.10
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = LibyaFocus.51 hours = 6 } }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = gratitude
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.50.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.50.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = nationalist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = LibyaFocus.53 hours = 3 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = LibyaFocus.50_tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			unlock_decision_tooltip = ITA_use_force_decision
			LBA = {
				add_ideas = LBA_treaty_of_benghazi
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFocus.50.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.50.c executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = LibyaFocus.52 hours = 6 } }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = insult
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFocus.93.b executed"
		trigger = { original_tag = MAU }
		if = {
			limit = {
				LBA = { has_country_flag = libya_casablanca_accords_signed_by_SHA }
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = SHA
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			add_state_core = 372
			add_state_core = 373
		}
		else = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = SHA
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LBA = { NOT = { has_country_flag = libya_casablanca_accords_signed_by_MOR } }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				target = MOR
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

			FROM = { add_ideas = LBA_chad_trade_deal_libya }

#Anti-Black riots - Random/repeating
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.2
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.2.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.2.d
	picture = GFX_generic_islamic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_idea = LBA_stream_of_refugees
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = LBA_minority_rights
				has_completed_focus = LBA_minority_protection
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_country_flag = LBA_black_people_favoured
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_idea = LBA_treaty_of_benghazi
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_completed_focus = LBA_utilise_toubou
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_completed_focus = LBA_strip_toubou_of_citizenship
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.2.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		increase_policing_budget = yes
		block_police_decrease = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.2.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.2.b executed"

	trigger = {
		date > 2001.01.01
		has_idea = international_sanctions
		is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_active_mission = libya_negotiations_with_un
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.6.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.6.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 10 }
		change_fossil_fuel_industry_opinion = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = libya_negotiations_with_un
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = libya_negotiations_with_un
				days = -60
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LBA_shukri_ghanem_prime_minister
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.6.b

		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = LBA_opec_research_expert
			bonus = 0.20
			uses = 2
			category = CAT_excavation_tech
			category = Cat_FUEL_OIL
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.6.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.6.c executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		increase_economic_growth = yes
	}

		}

				has_active_mission = libya_negotiations_with_un

			}

			target = BUL
			modifier = note_of_protest
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = BUL
			modifier = note_of_protest

			limit = { NOT = { has_government = fascism } }

					country_event = { id = LibyaRandomEvents.11 days = 30 }

country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.15
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.15.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.15.d
	picture = GFX_weapons_arms1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			SNA = { has_war_with = SHB }
			SOM = { has_war_with = SHB }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_completed_focus = LBA_destability_somalia
		}
	}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.15.a executed"

				target = SNA
				modifier = military_deals
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SNA
				modifier = military_deals
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ROOT.influence_target = SOM }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOM
				modifier = military_deals
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOM
				modifier = military_deals
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 4 }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		set_temp_variable = { ROOT.influence_target = SHB }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -4 }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SHB
			modifier = rebel_support
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SHB
			modifier = rebel_support

				target = SNA

		}

				target = SOM
				modifier = rebel_support
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOM
				modifier = rebel_support
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -4 }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		set_temp_variable = { ROOT.influence_target = SHB }

			target = SHB

#LIFG assassinated leader - Random/repeating
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.24
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.24.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.24.d
	picture = GFX_gulf_terror

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		fascism > 0.20
		NOT = { has_government = fascism }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = LBA_peace_with_lifg }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			has_idea = police_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_idea = police_03
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_idea = police_04
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			has_idea = police_05
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_completed_focus = LBA_ignore_lifg
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.24.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.24.a executed"
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Muammar Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = muammar_gaddafi_dead
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Muhammad Muammar Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dead
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Saif al-Islam Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = saif_al_islam_gaddafi_dead
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Al-Saadi Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = al_saadi_gaddafi_dead
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Mutassim Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_dead
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Hannibal Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = hannibal_gaddafi_dead
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Ayesha Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = ayesha_gaddafi_dead
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Saif al-Arab Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = saif_al_arab_gaddafi_dead
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Khamis Gaddafi"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = khamis_gaddafi_dead
			}
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		set_ruling_leader = yes
		set_leader = yes
	}

#Grand Mufti issues fatwa against government's enemies - Random/single
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.30
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.30.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.30.d
	picture = GFX_generic_islamic_rally

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = LBA_appoint_grand_mufti
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_government = fascism
					fascism < 0.50
				}
				AND = {
					has_government = communism
					communism < 0.50
				}
				AND = {
					has_government = neutrality
					neutrality < 0.50
				}
				AND = {
					has_government = democratic
					democratic < 0.50
				}
				AND = {
					has_government = nationalist
					nationalist < 0.50
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.30.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.30.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = nationalist
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
	}

}

	title = LibyaRandomEvents.33.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.33.d
	picture = GFX_iraq_war3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_government = fascism
		has_completed_focus = LBA_join_sahel_war
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.33.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.33.a executed"
		add_war_support = 0.025
		add_manpower = 250
	}

}

#Teacher's protest biased education - Random/repeating
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.35
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.35.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.35.d
	picture = GFX_african_school

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = LBA_religious_education
			has_completed_focus = LBA_national_education
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.35.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.35.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_stability = -0.025
		decrease_education_budget = yes
		block_edu_increase = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.35.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.35.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.35.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.35.c executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_stability = 0.025
		increase_education_budget = yes
		block_edu_decrease = yes
	}

}

#Ba'athist support abroad - Random/repeating
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.38
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.38.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.38.d
	picture = GFX_generic_islamic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = LBA_appoint_baathist_advisor
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.38.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.38.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_the_middle_east = yes
					has_idea = sunni
				}
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.38.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.38.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_the_middle_east = yes
					has_idea = sunni
				}
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
	}

}

#Ba'athist resistance abroad - Random/repeating
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.39
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.39.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.39.d
	picture = GFX_generic_islamic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = LBA_appoint_baathist_advisor
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.39.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.39.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_arabic_nation = yes
						is_middle_eastern_nation = yes
					}
					OR = {
						has_idea = sunni
						has_idea = shia
						has_idea = sufi_islam
						has_idea = ibadi
					}
					is_influencer = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -4 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.39.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.39.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_arabic_nation = yes
						is_middle_eastern_nation = yes
					}
					OR = {
						has_idea = sunni
						has_idea = shia
						has_idea = sufi_islam
						has_idea = ibadi
					}
					is_influencer = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
	}

}

	id = LibyaRandomEvents.44
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.44.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.44.d
	picture = GFX_politics_surveillence

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = LBA_empowered_revolutionary_committees
			has_idea = LBA_general_peoples_congress
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			has_idea = LBA_empowered_revolutionary_committees
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.44.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.44.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_stability = 0.025
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.44.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.44.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_intelligence_community_opinion = yes
	}

}

	}

		modify_treasury_effect = yes
	}

}

#Royal invests in another country - Random/repeating

	id = LibyaRandomEvents.51
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.51.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.51.d
	picture = GFX_united_states_dollar

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_idea = LBA_royal_family_returned_2
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.51.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.51.a executed"
		set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = gdp_total }
		multiply_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 0.02 }
		modify_international_investment_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_the_middle_east = yes
					has_idea = sunni
				}
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
	}

}

#Mercenaries accused of war crimes - Random/repeating
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.58
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.58.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.58.d
	picture = GFX_event_pmcs

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = LBA_central_african_mercs
			has_completed_focus = LBA_send_mercenaries
		}
		is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country = {
				has_volunteers_amount_from = {
					tag = LBA
					count > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.58.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.58.a executed"
		add_political_power = -200
	}

}

#Mercenaries bring back experience - Random/repeating
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.59
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.59.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.59.d
	picture = GFX_event_pmcs

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = LBA_central_african_mercs
			has_completed_focus = LBA_send_mercenaries
		}
		is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country = {
				has_volunteers_amount_from = {
					tag = LBA
					count > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.59.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.59.a executed"
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
					name = LBA_lessons_from_veterans
					cost_reduction = 0.15
					uses = 1
					category = CAT_land_doctrine
				}
			}
			10 = {
				add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
					name = LBA_lessons_from_veterans
					cost_reduction = 0.15
					uses = 1
					category = CAT_air_doctrine
				}
			}
			10 = {

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			has_idea = unrestrained_corruption
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_idea = rampant_corruption
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			has_idea = crippling_corruption
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_idea = paralyzing_corruption
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.62.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.62.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_political_power = -200
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_fossil_fuel_industry_opinion = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.62.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.62.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { original_tag = ROOT }
				any_owned_state = {
					oil > 0
				}
				NOT = { has_idea = non_power }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = THIS }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}
		libya_decrease_nationalisation_5 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_fossil_fuel_industry_opinion = yes
	}

}

		}

			factor = 0.7

		}

#Toubou Rebellion - Random/repeating
country_event = {
	id = LibyaRandomEvents.67
	title = LibyaRandomEvents.67.t
	desc = LibyaRandomEvents.67.d
	picture = GFX_liberate_minorities

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { country_exists = TIE }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = LBA_strip_toubou_of_citizenship }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = LBA_minority_rights }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = LBA_minority_protection }
		OR = {
			has_civil_war = yes
			has_war_with = TRP
			has_war_with = CYR
			has_war_with = FEZ
		}
		OR = {
			owns_state = 1100
			owns_state = 920
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		release = TIE
		hidden_effect = {
			transfer_units_fraction = {
				target = TIE
				size = 0.01
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = LBA_unit_leader_trait_tripolitania
						has_trait = LBA_unit_leader_trait_tuareg
					}
				}
			}
			TIE = {
				load_oob = "TIE_rebellion"
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = LBA_unit_leader_trait_toubou
			}
			set_nationality = TIE
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.67.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.67.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = yes
				surrender_progress > 0.25
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { loyalty_change = -0.10 }
		libya_change_tripolitania_loyalty = yes
		libya_change_cyrenaica_loyalty = yes
		libya_change_fezzan_loyalty = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = LBA
					AND = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = CYR
							original_tag = FEZ
						}
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TIE
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaRandomEvents.67.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaRandomEvents.67.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = yes
				surrender_progress > 0.25
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = LibyaTribes.6
	title = LibyaTribes.6.t
	desc = LibyaTribes.6.d
	picture = GFX_libyan_tribes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_disabled }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_tripolitanian_offender
				}
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_cyrenaican_offender
				}
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_fezzani_offender
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaTribes.6.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaTribes.6.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_political_power = 150
		set_temp_variable_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		libya_increase_loyalty_single_offender = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaTribes.6.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaTribes.6.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_temp_variable_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		libya_decrease_loyalty_single_offender = yes
	}
}

#Tribal elder suspected of treason

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_disabled }

	}

			random_list = {
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_tripolitanian_offender
				}
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_cyrenaican_offender
				}
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_fezzani_offender
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaTribes.7.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaTribes.7.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_intelligence_community_opinion = yes
		libya_increase_loyalty_single_offender = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaTribes.7.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaTribes.7.b executed"

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_intelligence_community_opinion = yes
		libya_decrease_loyalty_single_offender = yes
	}

					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_tripolitanian_offender
				}
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_cyrenaican_offender
				}
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = LBA_tribalism_fezzani_offender
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaTribes.8.a

		multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 0.02 }

	option = {
		name = LibyaTribes.8.b

		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		libya_decrease_loyalty_single_offender = yes
	}
}

#Death of Gaddafi's child
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFamily.1
	title = LibyaFamily.1.t
	desc = LibyaFamily.1.d
	picture = GFX_libya_gaddafi_family

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFamily.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFamily.1.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				 has_country_flag = kill_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi
				 NOT = { has_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dead }
			}
			retire_character = LBA_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dummy
			set_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dead
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kill_saif_al_islam_gaddafi
				NOT = { has_country_flag = saif_al_islam_gaddafi_dead }
			}
			retire_character = LBA_saif_al_islam_gaddafi_dummy
			set_country_flag = saif_al_islam_gaddafi_dead
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kill_al_saadi_gaddafi
				NOT = { has_country_flag = al_saadi_gaddafi_dead }
			}
			retire_character = LBA_al_saadi_gaddafi_dummy
			set_country_flag = al_saadi_gaddafi_dead
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kill_mutassim_gaddafi
				NOT = { has_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_dead }
			}
			retire_character = LBA_mutassim_gaddafi_dummy
			set_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_dead
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kill_hannibal_gaddafi
				NOT = { has_country_flag = hannibal_gaddafi_dead }
			}
			retire_character = LBA_hannibal_gaddafi_dummy
			set_country_flag = hannibal_gaddafi_dead
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kill_ayesha_gaddafi
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ayesha_gaddafi_dead }
			}
			retire_character = LBA_ayesha_gaddafi_dummy
			set_country_flag = ayesha_gaddafi_dead
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kill_saif_al_arab_gaddafi
				NOT = { has_country_flag = saif_al_arab_gaddafi_dead }
			}
			retire_character = LBA_saif_al_arab_gaddafi_dummy
			set_country_flag = saif_al_arab_gaddafi_dead
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kill_khamis_gaddafi
				NOT = { has_country_flag = khamis_gaddafi_dead }
			}
			retire_character = LBA_khamis_gaddafi_dummy
			set_country_flag = khamis_gaddafi_dead
		}
		set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 30 }
		libya_gaddafi_family_modify_instability = yes
		libya_find_next_gaddafi_heir = yes
		update_gaddafi_family_ideas = yes
	}
}

#Muhammad Muammar Gaddafi abuses power
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFamily.2
	title = LibyaFamily.2.t
	desc = LibyaFamily.2.d
	picture = GFX_libya_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes
		has_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_head_of_GPTC
		NOT = { has_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dead }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_exile }
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Muhammad Muammar Gaddafi"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaFamily.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFamily.2.a executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 20 }
		libya_gaddafi_family_modify_instability = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFamily.2.b

	title = LibyaFamily.3.t
	desc = LibyaFamily.3.d

	trigger = {
		is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes
		NOT = { has_idea = international_sanctions }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dead }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_exile }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_dead }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_exile }
	}

			custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_add_king_of_coke_tt
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFamily.3.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFamily.3.b executed"

		set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 20 }

			custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_add_king_of_coke_tt
		}
		set_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_king_of_coke
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFamily.3.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFamily.3.b executed"
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		random_list = {
			45 = {
				set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 10 }
				libya_gaddafi_family_modify_instability = yes
				LBA_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dummy = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_add_king_of_coke_tt
				}
				set_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_king_of_coke
				random = {
					chance = 25
					LBA_mutassim_gaddafi_dummy = { custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_killed_in_firefight_tt }
					set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 20 }
					libya_gaddafi_family_modify_instability = yes
					retire_character = LBA_mutassim_gaddafi_dummy
					set_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_dead
				}
				libya_find_next_gaddafi_heir = yes
				update_gaddafi_family_ideas = yes
			}
			45 = {
				set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 10 }
				libya_gaddafi_family_modify_instability = yes
				LBA_mutassim_gaddafi_dummy = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_add_king_of_coke_tt
				}
				set_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_king_of_coke
				random = {
					chance = 25
					LBA_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dummy = { custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_killed_in_firefight_tt }
					set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 20 }
					libya_gaddafi_family_modify_instability = yes
					retire_character = LBA_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dummy
					set_country_flag = muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dead
				}
				libya_find_next_gaddafi_heir = yes
				update_gaddafi_family_ideas = yes
			}
			10 = {
				LBA_mutassim_gaddafi_dummy = { custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_killed_in_firefight_tt }
				LBA_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dummy = { custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_killed_in_firefight_tt }
				set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 40 }
				libya_gaddafi_family_modify_instability = yes
				retire_character = LBA_mutassim_gaddafi_dummy
				set_country_flag = mutassim_gaddafi_dead
				retire_character = LBA_muhammad_muammar_gaddafi_dummy

				update_gaddafi_family_ideas = yes
			}
		}

			has_country_flag = al_saadi_gaddafi_playboy_lifestyle
		}
	}

		is_ruled_by_a_gaddafi = yes
		has_country_flag = al_saadi_gaddafi_substance_abuser

		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {

				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}

				custom_effect_tooltip = gaddafi_family_gain_convicted_criminal_tt
			}
		}

		name = LibyaFamily.46.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFamily.46.b executed"
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saif_al_arab_gaddafi_exile } }
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_temp_variable = { family_instability_change = 10 }

	}

			base = 50

				factor = 0
				has_idea = NATO_member
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = ITA }
			add_state_claim = 73
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = GER }
			add_state_claim = 74
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = FRA }
			add_state_claim = 72
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SWI
			modifier = called_for_our_destruction
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SWI
			modifier = called_for_our_destruction
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT }
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = LBA }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = LibyaFamily.72 hours = 6 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = LibyaFamily.71.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFamily.71.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = nationalist
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SWI
			modifier = diplomatic_support
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SWI
			modifier = diplomatic_support
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = LibyaFamily.73 hours = 6 } }
	}
}

	}
}

#Libya calls for the dismantling of Switzerland - Switzerland
country_event = {
	id = LibyaFamily.74
	title = LibyaFamily.74.t
	desc = LibyaFamily.74.d
	picture = GFX_libya_muammar_gaddafi

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LibyaFamily.74.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaFamily.74.a executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = diplomatic_support
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = diplomatic_support
			}
		}
	}
}

#Libyan National Democratic Front expands in Libya
country_event = {
	id = LibyaCivilWar.1
	title = LibyaCivilWar.1.t
	desc = LibyaCivilWar.1.d
	picture = GFX_politics_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = libya_gaddafi_family_anti_government_protests
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaCivilWar.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaCivilWar.1.a executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 3 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = USA }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				IRQ = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT }
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = IRQ }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}
	}
}

#Army ignores protesters
country_event = {
	id = LibyaCivilWar.6
	title = LibyaCivilWar.6.t
	desc = LibyaCivilWar.6.d
	picture = GFX_politics_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = libya_gaddafi_family_anti_government_protests
		OR = {
			has_idea = LBA_revolutionary_guard_corps
			has_idea = LBA_revolutionary_guard_corps_expanded
			has_idea = LBA_revolutionary_guard_corps_logistics
			has_idea = LBA_revolutionary_guard_corps_logistics_with_research
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaCivilWar.6.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaCivilWar.6.a executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 22 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = libya_gaddafi_family_anti_government_protests
			days = -15
		}
	}
}

#Pilots abandon the country
country_event = {
	id = LibyaCivilWar.13
	title = LibyaCivilWar.13.t
	desc = LibyaCivilWar.13.d
	picture = GFX_politics_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = libya_gaddafi_family_anti_government_protests
		OR = {
			has_equipment = {
				small_plane_airframe_1 > 5
			}
			has_equipment = {
				small_plane_strike_airframe_1 > 5
			}
			has_equipment = {
				medium_plane_fighter_airframe_1 > 5
			}
		}
		country_exists = MLT
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaCivilWar.13.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaCivilWar.13.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_equipment = {
					small_plane_airframe_1 > 5
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = small_plane_airframe_1
				amount = 5
				target = MLT
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_equipment = {
					small_plane_strike_airframe_1 > 5
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = small_plane_strike_airframe_1
				amount = 5
				target = MLT
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_equipment = {
					medium_plane_fighter_airframe_1 > 5
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = medium_plane_fighter_airframe_1
				amount = 5
				target = MLT
			}
		}
	}
}

#Sailors abandon the country
country_event = {
	id = LibyaCivilWar.14
	title = LibyaCivilWar.14.t
	desc = LibyaCivilWar.14.d
	picture = GFX_politics_protest

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = libya_gaddafi_family_anti_government_protests
		OR = {
			has_navy_size = {
				size > 0
				archetype = corvette
			}
			has_navy_size = {
				size > 0
				archetype = attack_submarine
			}
		}
		country_exists = ITA
	}

	option = {
		name = LibyaCivilWar.14.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: LibyaCivilWar.14.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_navy_size = {
					size > 0
					archetype = corvette
				}
			}
			destroy_ships = {
				type = corvette
				count = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_navy_size = {
					size > 0
					archetype = attack_submarine
				}
			}
			destroy_ships = {
				type = attack_submarine
				count = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
